User<7363918317>: –¢9

Roman: Orkel (Facepunch Studios)  Nov 8, 2024, 12:07 GMT+1  Hello Roman,   If it changes vanilla gameplay, it is modded. Selling items, scrap, weapons, blueprints, and other gameplay bonuses etc to players affects vanilla gameplay and requires modded, even if the sales are done from a custom website or console. Selling or having skip server queues and colored names/name tags is allowed on community. Please read our article for the general guidelines. It is up to server owners to ensure that their servers are not changing vanilla gameplay. https://support.facepunchstudios.com/hc/en-us/articles/360009062817-Guidelines-for-community-servers-using-plugins-mods
